57542 - Jolly Salah: hatgib el cost le kol condition men el three eli 3andak as follows:
DNUM = DNUMBER => Nested loops with Dept. as outer loop
=> Nested loops with Proj. as outer loop
=> Single loop with Proj. as outer loop
MGRSSN = SSN => Nested loops with Emp. as outer loop
=> Nested loops with Dept. as outer loop
PLOCATION = 'Stafford' => Using the calculation for the equality condition of the secondary index


el 7all da kollena ettafa2na 3alih w Lydia ba3atet sa2alet Caroline this solution and Caroline approved !
